<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AI集成的无线接入网（AI-RAN）中，由于存在大量并发的xApps/rApps，参数与KPI之间的依赖关系是动态变化的。现有的监控手段无法实时验证系统所假设的依赖关系在当前运行环境下是否依然有效，导致难以进行准确的冲突监控与诊断。

Method: 提出了一种基于布尔矩阵乘法的轻量级监控原语。该方法通过滑动窗口机制，对比近期参数-活动和KPI响应事件与当前依赖估计的一致性，仅在结构发生改变时触发重新计算，从而实现对依赖关系的动态追踪。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在受控的布尔事件流中，即使存在布尔观测噪声，仍能高效、准确地追踪依赖关系的变化，验证了该方案在处理动态网络结构演变方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的轻量级布尔矩阵追踪方法能够有效识别AI-RAN中应用参数与KPI之间的依赖关系变化。该机制作为一种可解释的信号，能为复杂网络环境下的冲突诊断和模型迭代提供可靠支撑，且在噪声环境下表现出良好的鲁棒性和效率。

Abstract: Future AI-integrated Radio Access Networks (AI-RAN) will combine open programmability with learning-enabled xApps, rApps, and control functions that act on shared parameters and key performance indicators (KPIs). For conflict monitoring, it is not enough to know which applications are deployed; the system must also know whether the parameter--KPI dependencies assumed by runtime diagnosis remain valid under the current operating regime. This paper studies a lightweight monitoring primitive for that purpose: tracking an interpretable dependency representation from streaming telemetry events.
  We represent active dependencies by a Boolean matrix and use Boolean matrix multiplication to check whether recent parameter-activity and KPI-response events are consistent with the current estimate. We propose a sliding-window inference procedure that reuses the estimate when it remains consistent and recomputes it when recent observations indicate structural change. The tracker is intended as an explainable signal for conflict diagnosis and slow-loop model refresh, not as an autonomous mitigation mechanism. Experiments on controlled Boolean event streams show efficient and accurate tracking under dependency changes and Boolean observation noise.

</details>


### [127] [Uncertainty-Aware LLM-Guided Policy Shaping for Sparse-Reward Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06673)
*Ujjwal Bhatta,Utsabi Dangol,Sumaly Bajracharya,Rodrigue Rizk,KC Santosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ULPS框架通过将大语言模型与不确定性感知机制融入强化学习训练，利用A*符号轨迹引导和自适应策略平衡，有效解决了稀疏奖励环境下的探索与收敛难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对强化学习中稀疏奖励和异构任务序列导致的收敛缓慢、泛化能力弱及探索效率低下等挑战，旨在通过大语言模型（LLM）提供结构化的行为引导，提升学习性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为ULPS的新框架：1. 使用基于A*的预言机合成最优符号轨迹并以此微调BERT模型；2. 在训练期间，利用Monte Carlo (MC) dropout估计认知不确定性，并根据该不确定性调整语言模型的行动建议权重；3. 通过基于熵的混合机制自适应地平衡LLM引导与PPO学习策略，实现先验知识与策略灵活性的协同。

Result: 在MiniGridUnlockPickup基准测试中，ULPS在成功率、奖励效率和样本复杂度方面均优于现有基线。执行准确率提升超过9%，有效降低了环境交互次数，并获得了更高的奖励曲线下面积（AUC）。

Conclusion: ULPS通过整合符号轨迹、预训练语言先验和不确定性感知控制，为稀疏奖励下的多任务强化学习提供了一种鲁棒且高效的通用框架，并具有在复杂环境（如部分可观测或多智能体）中的扩展潜力。

Abstract: Sparse rewards and heterogeneous task sequences remain persistent challenges in Reinforcement Learning (RL), often resulting in slow convergence, weak generalization, and inefficient exploration. We propose Uncertainty-Aware LLM-Guided Policy Shaping (ULPS), a novel framework that integrates a calibrated Large Language Model (LLM) into the RL training loop to provide structured, uncertainty-modulated behavioral guidance. ULPS employs an A*-based oracle to synthesize optimal symbolic trajectories, which are used to fine-tune a BERT-based language model. During training, this model supplies action suggestions whose influence is conditioned on epistemic uncertainty estimated via Monte Carlo (MC) dropout. An entropy-based blending mechanism adaptively balances LLM guidance and the learned policy (via Proximal Policy Optimization, PPO), allowing the agent to prioritize reliable priors while preserving adaptability. We evaluate ULPS on the MiniGridUnlockPickup benchmark and observe consistent improvements in success rate, reward efficiency, and sample complexity over unguided, uncalibrated, and standard RL baselines. ULPS achieves more than 9% improvement in execution accuracy after fine-tuning, requires fewer environment interactions, and yields higher reward AUC. Our results demonstrate that integrating symbolic A* trajectories, pretrained language priors, and uncertainty-aware control offers a principled and effective approach to multi-task reinforcement learning in sparse-reward domains, with potential extensibility to partially observable and multi-agent settings.

### [128] [Spatiotemporal Imputation with Graph-Informed Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06682)
*Zepeng Zhang,Aref Einizade,Jhony H. Giraldo,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GiFlow 是一种新型时空数据插补框架，通过利用图信息先验和流匹配技术，在保持高性能的同时提高了推理效率，解决了现有方法在误差传播和生成过程上的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的时空数据插补方法（如 RNN、GNN）存在误差累积问题，而现有的扩散模型方法虽缓解了误差累积，但存在采样效率低且依赖通用的高斯先验，难以充分利用时空数据特定的分布特性。

Method: 提出了 GiFlow 框架，核心包括：1. 构建图信息先验（Graph-informed prior），通过对可观测信号进行时空滤波，简化生成轨迹；2. 采用流匹配（Flow Matching）技术替代传统扩散模型；3. 设计混合向量场模型，集成空间注意力、时间注意力和时空传播机制，联合建模时空依赖。

Result: 在多个合成数据集和真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，GiFlow 在时空数据插补任务中表现优于当前最先进的（SOTA）方法。

Conclusion: GiFlow 通过引入图信息先验和高效的流匹配框架，有效克服了传统时空插补方法中误差累积和迭代采样效率低的问题，为处理时空缺失数据提供了更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Missing data is a common challenge in spatiotemporal systems, arising in applications such as air quality monitoring and urban traffic management. Traditional machine learning approaches, like recurrent and graph neural networks, rely on iterative propagation, which tends to accumulate errors over time and space. Recent diffusion-based methods mitigate error propagation but require iterative sampling and often depend on problem-agnostic Gaussian priors, limiting both efficiency and effectiveness. To address these limitations, we propose GiFlow, a Graph-Informed Flow Matching framework for spatiotemporal imputation. GiFlow replaces the typical Gaussian prior with a graph-informed prior constructed via spatiotemporal filtering of observable signals, which better aligns the source distribution to the target and thereby simplifies the generation trajectory. The flow field is parameterized by a hybrid vector field model that integrates spatial attention, temporal attention, and spatiotemporal propagation, enabling joint modeling of spatial and temporal dependencies. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that the proposed GiFlow outperforms the state-of-the-art approaches in spatiotemporal imputation. The code is available at https://github.com/zepengzhang/GiFlow.

### [129] [Towards Serverless Semi-Decentralized Federated Learning with Heterogeneous Optimizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06687)
*Su Wang,Mung Chiang,H. Vincent Poor*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 SSD-FL 框架，通过引入一种基于共识差距的轻量级聚类方法，成功优化了去中心化联邦学习在面对异构优化器和复杂网络结构时的收敛性能与通信开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在去中心化联邦学习环境中，现有的聚类方法研究尚浅。由于网络图结构、本地数据分布以及本地机器学习优化器的复杂耦合关系，如何在无中心服务器的情况下实现高效的聚类以提升可扩展性和资源利用率成为亟待解决的难题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SSD-FL 的无服务器半去中心化联邦学习框架。该方法通过一次性的轻量级设备间（D2D）初始化阶段实现自动聚类；利用引入“有效损失函数”将异构优化器与图正则化结合；基于 Cheeger 不等式通过评估共识差距，提出了一种迭代聚类算法，并推导出相应的收敛与共识界。

Result: 实验结果表明，与现有的三种去中心化联邦学习方法相比，SSD-FL 在多种网络拓扑结构、数据集以及不同的本地优化器设置下，均表现出更快的收敛速度和更高的通信效率。

Conclusion: SSD-FL 通过创新的聚类机制有效解决了去中心化联邦学习中异构优化器与网络结构耦合带来的挑战，在保证全局收敛性的同时，显著提升了通信效率和收敛速度。

Abstract: We investigate cluster formation, involving the number and composition of clusters, in decentralized federated learning (FL) with heterogeneous machine learning (ML) optimizers. While clustering in centralized FL has enabled scalability and resource savings, its value and development in fully decentralized environments have yet to be explored. Optimizing cluster formation in such environments is challenging, especially due to the complex coupling between network graph structures, local data heterogeneity, and different local ML model optimizers. To address these challenges, we propose serverless semi-decentralized FL (SSD-FL), a methodology requiring no persistent server infrastructure. In SSD-FL, cluster formation occurs via a lightweight, one-time device-to-device (D2D) initialization phase, after which actual ML model training (alongside consensus and convergence processes) is fully serverless. Functionally, SSD-FL segments global rounds into intra-cluster and inter-cluster regimes, ensuring global convergence and consensus through novel "effective loss functions" that integrate device-specific ML optimizers with network graph-based regularization. Next, SSD-FL leverages the consensus gap via the Cheeger inequality to develop an iterative clustering algorithm evaluated against our derived convergence and consensus bounds, which incorporate a unique scoring metric to quantify data and optimizer heterogeneity across devices. Finally, experimental evaluation against three categories of decentralized FL methodologies validate that SSD-FL improves both convergence speeds and communication efficiency across various network graphs, datasets, and local optimizer regimes.

### [130] [The Geography of Algorithmic Judgment: LLM Intermediaries, Place Identity, and Racial Steering in Housing Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06694)
*Hana Samad,Trung Lam,Christoph Mügge-Durum,Michael Akinwumi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了大型语言模型在住房搜索中存在基于种族身份的推荐偏差（种族引导），该偏差由用户背景、偏好表述与模型对城市空间的认知交互所致，强调了在住房AI应用中引入本地化与领域监管的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型正日益成为住房搜索的重要中介，但既有研究表明其在地理空间推荐中可能存在“种族引导”（Racial Steering）偏见。本研究旨在探讨这种引导行为的产生机制，以及模型如何解读不同用户的偏好，从而评估其对公平住房的影响。

Method: 研究团队对七种开源和闭源的大型语言模型进行了行为审计。实验涵盖了美国四个城市，采用了三种迭代提示条件（逐渐增加生活方式偏好背景），并模拟了公平住房领域的“配对测试”方法，以考察模型在不同用户身份和偏好下的推荐偏差。

Result: 研究发现，种族引导是模型解释性行为的一种涌现属性。测试表明，当增加生活方式偏好条件时，模型表现出的引导行为往往会增强或重构，这暗示模型可能根据用户种族身份对同一住房偏好做出不同解释。此外，研究证明城市环境对模型评估有显著影响，单一市场的测试结果无法简单推广到其他城市。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在住房推荐中存在“种族引导”现象，且这种行为并非静态属性，而是由用户身份、偏好表达与模型对城市空间的内置逻辑交互产生的结果。由于城市空间具有独特性，缺乏统一性，因此在住房等领域应用AI时，必须引入领域专家和本地化监管，以确保符合公平住房的相关法律和制度承诺。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly assuming an intermediary role in housing search through the integration of listing platforms within conversational interfaces, mediating access to information, search, and recommendations within urban settings. We expand on prior work on racial steering in LLMs by conducting a behavioral audit of seven open-weight and closed-source LLMs across four U.S. cities, testing location recommendations across three iterative prompting conditions that progressively add lifestyle preference context and reflect fair housing paired-testing methodologies. We find that steering is an emergent behavior of the model's interpretive license rather than primarily a static property. Steering results from the interaction of a user's identity, preference articulation, and the spatial logic that a model has internalized about learned representations of place, preference, and opportunity in a given city, and how different types of users relate to it. While steering was present, it was not uniform in direction or magnitude across evaluated conditions. Preference-conditioned testing often increased or reconfigured the number of models that exhibited steering behaviors relative to baseline conditions, suggesting that LLMs may interpret what the same housing preference means differently depending on the racial identity of the user. Our findings also demonstrate that the city is not a neutral testing unit for LLM evaluation in place-based sectors, and results from one local market cannot be assumed to generalize to another. Local and domain expertise will be required in the housing sector to ensure that legal and institutional commitments to fair housing are not undermined while adopting AI tools that mediate spatial access.

*Harsh Deshpande,Kushal Chawla,Sangwoo Cho,William Campbell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究提出了 RECAP 基准，旨在评估智能体在生产环境中面对瞬时变化约束时的“先发制人”适应能力；实验发现现有主流的提示优化方法在应对此类动态场景时均表现不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体系统基准测试多假设约束条件是静态的，或依赖被动式协议（通过评估反馈进行调整）。然而，生产环境中的智能体经常面临约束条件的即时变化（如政策更新或阈值调整），且基本不允许出现错误。目前缺乏能够衡量这种“先发制人式适应”能力的基准。

Method: 提出了 RECAP 基准测试，采用“先适应后测试”的严格协议。该基准要求提示优化方法在仅给定约束条件规范的情况下，必须在接触任何测试数据之前完成泛化，从而测量持续学习现象（如遗忘、回归和前向迁移）。

Result: 在跨 4 个大语言模型和 3 种调度策略的评估中，6 种现有的优化方法均未显示出显著的性能提升，且往往伴随着更高的延迟，证明了现有方法在先发制人式范式下的局限性。

Conclusion: 目前的提示工程（Prompt Engineering）优化方法主要针对静态或被动式场景，无法有效应对生产环境中即时、主动的约束变化。该研究强调了开发能够适应动态部署需求的先发制人式提示适应方法的紧迫性。

Abstract: Production agentic systems routinely face evolving constraints and must comply from the very next interaction. Scenarios like a tool-call notification changing a compliance threshold or a policy update adding disclosure requirements fit this criteria, having close to no room for errors in production. This proactive adaptation setting is common in deployment, but absent from current benchmarks, which assume either static constraint sets or reactive protocols with evaluation feedback. We introduce RECAP, a benchmark that measures continual-learning phenomena (forgetting, regression, forward transfer) at the constraint level under a strictly proactive adapt-then-test protocol: prompt optimization methods receive only the constraint specification and must generalize before seeing any test data. Evaluating six methods across four LLMs and three schedules with evolving constraints, we find that these methods show no significant improvement in performance, even after incurring a higher latency. These methods, designed for offline or reactive settings, are inadequate for the proactive paradigm. Our work emphasizes the growing need for designing proactive prompt adaptation methods, where the models must remain robust to evolving needs in deployment.

Abstract: While generative AI models have demonstrated remarkable success in structure-based drug design, they predominantly rely on deep binding pockets and struggle to sample effective ligands for challenging low-pocketability targets, such as the historically "undruggable" oncology targets KRAS and MYC. To address this gap, we introduce ShallowBench, a strictly curated benchmark of 5,780 shallow-pocket targets extracted from CrossDocked2020. By computing the difference between an Alpha Shape "lid" volume and the underlying protein atom voxel volume, we successfully isolated targets with low concavity while ensuring sufficient surface area for binding. Evaluating various state-of-the-art generative models reveals weaker predicted binding affinity on these low-concavity interfaces. ShallowBench therefore provides a rigorous benchmark for generative biology models and highlights the necessity of new architectural innovations or loss functions capable of navigating these challenging targets.

Electrocardiography (ECG) provides a low-cost and widely available tool for detecting these abnormalities, but ECG-based detection remains challenging due to heterogeneous lead-dependent manifestations, high-dimensional multi-lead signals, class imbalance, and the limited interpretability of deep learning models. We propose a multi-scale attention-enhanced convolutional network (MSAIC-Net) for ECG-based myocardial substrate abnormality detection. MSAIC-Net employs parallel atrous convolutional branches to extract ECG features across multiple temporal receptive fields. %, enabling the model to capture both local and longer-range temporal patterns. Channel attention is then used to adaptively reweight informative lead-wise and feature-channel representations. To address class imbalance and improve feature separability, we introduce a novel imbalance-aware supervised contrastive learning strategy that encourages samples from the same class to form compact representations while increasing separation between abnormal and normal samples. Lead-wise permutation importance is further incorporated to quantify the contribution of each ECG lead and improve model interpretability. The proposed method was evaluated on two complementary datasets: a low-data institutional cohort from the University of Virginia (UVA) Health System for myocardial scar classification and the large-scale public PTB-XL dataset from PhysioNet for MI identification. ### [134] [Flatland: The Adventures of Gradient Descent with Large Step Sizes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06722)
*Leonardo Galli,Curtis Fox,Wiebke Bartolomaeus,Mark Schmidt,Holger Rauhut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了神经网络训练中确定“大”步长的新准则，通过设计自适应优化方法使算法在训练全程保持在“稳定性边缘”之上，从而在提升收敛速度的同时优化模型的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度学习中，目标函数往往不是全局L-平滑的，这使得确定保证梯度下降收敛的最大步长成为一个长期悬而未决的理论和实践难题。该论文旨在解决这一难题，并探索大步长对收敛及泛化性能的影响。

Method: 提出了一种新的“大”步长定义，仅需梯度满足局部Lipschitz或Hölder连续性；设计了能够自动实现大步长的自适应一阶优化方法；利用“稳定性边缘（EoS）”理论，使算法在训练过程中动态调节步长，并始终保持在EoS阈值之上。

Result: 该方法成功证明了可以在训练初期即达到“稳定性边缘”；通过该方法，不仅能保证收敛，还能将损失函数的尖锐度（Hessian矩阵最大特征值）降至全局最小值；实验结果显示，该方法能够显著改善训练失败的情况，使其转变为高效的训练过程。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在神经网络训练中，允许梯度下降算法在训练初期进入稍微更陡峭的区域（处于“稳定性边缘”之上）反而能改善收敛速度并提高泛化能力。此外，过早地陷入全局平坦区域并不利于训练，通过自稳定机制，可以有效提升模型训练的成功率。

Abstract: The training of neural networks often entails objective functions that are not globally $L$-smooth. For these functions, it is both theoretically and practically difficult to reply to the question: what is the largest possible step size that ensures the convergence of gradient descent (GD)? We address this longstanding open question in deep learning by providing a unifying definition of "large" step sizes that requires only local Lipschitz (or even Hölder) continuity of the gradient. We design first-order adaptive methods that provably yield large step sizes and show that they operate at the edge of stability (EoS) right from the start of the training. In particular, the loss decreases nonmonotonically and the product between the step size and sharpness, i.e., the largest eigenvalue of the Hessian, stays above the EoS threshold of 2 throughout training. Using our method, we are also able to minimize the sharpness all the way down to its global minimum. Contrary to expectation, we find that encountering globally-flat regions too early in the training may both slow down convergence and jeopardize the generalization ability of the network. Exploiting a self-stabilization argument, we allow GD to enter slightly sharper valleys and turn unsuccessful training runs into very successful ones.

</details>


### [135] [Synthics: Synthetic Physics-like Datasets for Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06724)
*Jari Vepsäläinen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法生成高质量物理合成回归数据集的方法。该方法通过模拟物理方程的结构与约束，生成的合成数据在统计特性和下游机器学习任务表现上均能媲美真实数据，有效解决了物理科学领域数据稀缺的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习模型严重依赖于具有代表性的高质量数据，但在现实场景中，获取大规模且高质量的物理数据集往往成本高昂或不可行。因此，需要一种能够生成在结构和统计学上均能忠实反映物理规律的合成数据集的方法，以支持模型的训练与优化。

Method: 1. 采用贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法（BPCFG）来捕捉物理方程库的代数结构并采样生成新方程；2. 通过非侵入式探测（non-intrusive probing）界定每个方程的物理有效域并提取变量间的约束；3. 结合均匀分布和截断正态分布对有效域进行子范围采样，以模拟真实的实验条件；4. 使用柯尔莫哥洛夫-斯米尔诺夫检验（KS检验）进行统计验证。

Result: 1. 生成的合成方程在8个结构特征上均与费曼方程库相匹配，远优于未经平滑处理的纯概率文法（仅匹配2个）；2. 在超参数优化任务中，使用该合成数据训练的模型表现出色，平均排名达到前30%（第6/20名），显著优于使用随机表达式树（第10名）或噪声数据（第19名）的效果。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了利用贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法（BPCFG）生成的合成数据能够高度拟合物理方程的代数结构。这种方法不仅在统计学上与真实的费曼数据集高度一致，而且在实际的机器学习任务（如超参数优化）中，其表现与使用真实数据进行训练的效果相当，有效缓解了数据稀缺问题。

Abstract: Representative data is fundamental in machine learning, as limited data hinders generalisation. Collecting sufficient real-world samples is often infeasible. Synthetic data generation offers a practical solution, but only if the generated data faithfully reflects the structure of real observations. In this paper, a method for generating synthetic regression datasets that structurally resemble physics equations from a given equation corpus is presented. The approach uses a Bayesian Probabilistic Context-Free Grammar to capture the underlying algebraic structure of the corpus, from which novel equations are sampled. To ensure the generated inputs lie within a physically meaningful domain, the applicability domain is characterised for each equation through non-intrusive probing, also recovering inter-variable constraints. Input sampling further mimics realistic experimental conditions by drawing from random sub-ranges of the valid domain with mixed uniform and truncated normal distributions. The generated data is statistically validated against the Feynman equation corpus using Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests. The generated equations match the corpus on all of the eight studied structural features, compared to only two for an unsmoothed purely probabilistic grammar, demonstrating that the Bayesian prior is essential for structural fidelity given the size of the corpus. In a downstream hyperparameter-tuning task, a gradient-boosted regressor tuned on the synthetic data picks, on average, the 6th-best configuration out of 20 on real data, matching the result of tuning on real data itself and substantially outperforming random expression trees (10th) and noise (19th).

</details>

*Yikai Zhang,Gaoxiang Jia,Jie Ding,Boxiang Wang*

TL;DR: TorchKM 是一个基于 GPU 加速的开源核机器算法库（包含 SVM、核逻辑回归等），通过优化线性代数运算提供 scikit-learn 风格的接口，大幅提升了模型训练与选择的计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的核方法（Kernel Machines）在处理大规模数据时受限于 CPU 的计算瓶颈，且缺乏高效、易用且具备 GPU 加速功能的开源实现，难以满足现代机器学习对计算效率的需求。

Method: 该库利用 PyTorch 的 GPU 计算能力，对核机器算法进行重新设计，采用 GPU 友好的线性代数实现，并通过智能重用矩阵运算来加速整个训练和模型选择流水线，同时保持与 scikit-learn 兼容的 API 风格。

Result: 基准测试表明，TorchKM 在保持模型预测性能与现有标准基准相当的前提下，在训练速度和模型选择效率上实现了显著提升。

Conclusion: TorchKM 提供了一个高效且易于使用的 GPU 加速核方法库，能够显著提升传统核算法（如 SVM、核逻辑回归等）在训练和模型选择阶段的性能，为大规模机器学习任务提供了实用工具。

Abstract: TorchKM is an open-source library for kernel machines, including support vector machines, kernel logistic regression, and kernel quantile regression, with GPU acceleration. The library features a scikit-learn-style API and is designed to exploit GPU-friendly linear algebra, accelerating the full training and model-selection pipeline through intelligent reuse of matrix operations. Benchmarks show competitive predictive performance together with substantial speedups over standard baselines. Code and documentation are available at https://github.com/YikaiZhang95/torchkm, and the package can be easily installed via PyPI.

</details>


### [137] [Learn to Match: Two-Sided Matching with Temporally Extended Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06744)
*Haijing Zong,Yancheng Liang,Boyang Zhou,Natasha Jaques*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对传统匹配模型忽略动态信息获取的缺陷，引入了一个基于 POMG 的动态匹配市场框架 Learn2Match，通过多智能体强化学习实验，揭示了该方法在提升社会福利方面的优势，并指出了当前算法在协作探索能力上的提升空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的匹配模型多将匹配过程简化为关于固定偏好的即时反馈，忽略了现实中匹配信息往往随时间推移（如面试、长期互动、学习等）而逐渐显露的动态特征，导致无法处理信息随时间变化并影响未来决策的复杂场景。

Method: 作者将双边匹配市场形式化为一个部分可观测马尔可夫博弈（POMG），包含昂贵的匹配前筛选、带噪声的匹配后观察、演化的潜在特征以及内生的持续或解除机制。同时，开发了 Learn2Match 多智能体强化学习基准测试平台，并对比了独立 PPO 算法与基准 Bandit 算法（CA-ETC）的表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，在具有时间扩展反馈的市场中，独立 PPO 算法相比传统的 Bandit 类算法（CA-ETC）能够实现更高的累积社会福利和更低的累积遗憾；但在信息摩擦损失方面表现较差，说明当前的 MARL 算法尚未完全具备匹配-老虎机方法所拥有的协调探索结构。

Conclusion: 本文提出了 Learn2Match 框架，证明了多智能体强化学习（MARL）在处理动态匹配市场方面具有巨大潜力，但也指出当前的端到端强化学习算法在协作探索和信息摩擦方面仍存在不足，未来的研究需将强化学习的适应性、多臂老虎机算法的统计严谨性以及稳定匹配机制的结构化洞察相结合。

Abstract: Two-sided matching markets often involve information that unfolds over time through interviews, repeated interaction, learning, and separation. Existing matching models typically reduce this process to immediate sub-Gaussian feedback about fixed preferences, missing settings where payoff-relevant information is revealed gradually and changes future matching decisions. We introduce a framework with temporally extended feedback, that formulates two-sided matching as a partially observable Markov game with costly pre-match screening, noisy post-match observations, evolving latent profiles, and endogenous continuation or dissolution. We instantiate this framework in Learn2Match, a multi-agent reinforcement-learning benchmark for dynamic matching markets. Learn2Match supports decentralized decision making over whom to interview, whom to match with, and when to dissolve a match, while evaluating policies using regret, social welfare, and an information-friction loss that measures the welfare gap caused by incomplete revelation of latent preferences. We find that independent PPO achieves higher cumulative social welfare and lower cumulative regret than the bandit-style CA-ETC baseline under temporally extended feedback, demonstrating the promise of MARL for dynamic matching markets. However, PPO still incurs higher information-friction loss, revealing that end-to-end MARL does not yet provide the coordinated exploration structure of matching-bandit methods. These results position Learn2Match as a benchmark for developing the next generation of matching-market algorithms: methods that are adaptive like RL agents, statistically disciplined like bandit algorithms, and structurally aware like stable-matching mechanisms.

### [138] [Performance Variation in Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06746)
*Haruto Tanaka,A. Rupam Mahmood*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对强化学习算法“运行间鲁棒性差”这一常被忽视的问题，本文批评了传统的均值评估法，并提出了一套基于百分位数的统计与可视化评估工具，能更真实地呈现算法性能的波动特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习算法在相同配置下进行多次独立运行（run-to-run）时，往往表现出显著的性能差异（即缺乏鲁棒性）。然而，现有的研究大多仅关注平均性能及其置信区间，这种做法掩盖了算法运行间的高波动性，导致研究结果存在误导性或低估了性能风险。

Method: 作者提出了一种替代性的基于百分位数的评估工具：1. 最小-最大区间四分位距（min-max IPR）统计量，用于量化性能变化范围；2. 运行级百分位数高亮（run-wise percentile highlighting）可视化方法，用于直观展示多组实验的性能分布及其不稳定性。

Result: 通过三个案例研究验证了该方法的有效性：发现层归一化（LayerNorm）能缩小PPO的性能差异；通过对比发现TD-MPC在保持最高数据效率的同时，表现出最小的性能波动；对比DQN与Rainbow在Atari环境中的表现，揭示了两者虽性能不同但面临类似的波动水平。

Conclusion: 本文指出，基于均值及其置信区间的传统评估方法无法充分揭示强化学习算法在不同运行间表现出的剧烈不稳定性（即性能差异）。作者提出的基于百分位数的统计与可视化方法，能够更稳健且直观地量化运行间的性能波动，有助于研究者更全面地评估算法的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Deep reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms often suffer from low run-to-run robustness, manifesting as significant performance variation across independent runs of identically configured agents. Although this issue poses a spectrum of challenges across research and practice, relatively few studies develop methods to evaluate it; RL research instead often reports uncertainty in the estimated mean performance. In this paper, we outline the limitations of conventional uncertainty and variation estimates, particularly their misalignment with purpose and the risk of underreporting. We then propose an alternative percentile-based statistic and visualization method, min-max IPR and run-wise percentile highlighting, respectively. These percentile-based tools are easy to interpret and rely on standard properties of sample percentiles, providing rich information about run-to-run performance variation. We demonstrate this through three case studies. First, we show that LayerNorm and penultimate-layer normalizations narrow performance variation in PPO, whereas the variation is mostly unchanged in SAC. Second, we compare PPO, SAC, TD-MPC, and TD-MPC2, and show TD-MPC exhibits the least variation while being the most data efficient among the four. Finally, in a comparison of DQN and Rainbow on five Atari environments, we show that both algorithms exhibit similar levels of performance variation.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非合同制服务环境下，流失行为无法被直接观测，现有方法往往依赖于简化的时间假设或单点行为表示，难以满足持续性风险评估、可解释性以及实际部署的需求。

Method: 提出了一种时间明确的流失预测框架，通过滚动行为窗口（30天观测期+30天评估期）建模客户行为，实现了基于特征工程和序列化建模的统一时间设计，能够支持持续的风险评估。

Result: 在真实大型数据集上，基于特征的模型准确率达到87.6%，ROC-AUC为0.94；基于序列的模型召回率高达96.1%；且在无需重训练的情况下，面对时间偏移仍能保持83%以上的准确率及0.91以上的ROC-AUC。

Conclusion: 研究表明，严谨的时间窗口设计比单纯追求模型复杂度对于实现稳健、可解释且易于部署的流失预测更为关键，为动态服务环境下的决策支持提供了实践基础。

Abstract: Customer churn prediction is a central task in customer analytics, particularly in non-contractual, pay-per-use service environments where disengagement is not explicitly observed and must be inferred from behavioral inactivity. Existing churn prediction approaches often rely on simplified temporal assumptions or single-point representations of customer behavior, which limit their ability to support continuous risk assessment, interpretability, and realistic deployment over time. This study proposes a temporally explicit churn prediction framework that models customer behavior using rolling behavioral windows, enabling repeated and instance-level churn risk estimation as customer activity evolves. Customer behavior is summarized within a fixed 30-day observation window, followed by a 30-day future churn evaluation window, ensuring a clear temporal separation between behavioral evidence and churn outcomes. The framework integrates feature-based and sequence-based learning approaches within a unified temporal design. The proposed approach is evaluated on a large-scale, real-world dataset from a non-contractual service platform. Empirical results demonstrate strong and stable predictive performance, with accuracy reaching 87.6% and ROC-AUC of 0.94 for the feature-based model, while the sequence-based model achieves recall as high as 96.1% by capturing temporal disengagement patterns. Evaluation on future unseen data confirms meaningful robustness under temporal shift, with accuracy remaining above 83% and ROC-AUC exceeding 0.91 without model retraining. Overall, the findings highlight that carefully designed temporal framing, rather than model complexity alone, is critical for achieving robust, interpretable, and deployment-ready churn prediction. The study provides a practical foundation for churn-oriented decision support in dynamic service environments.

### [141] [Interpreting Learning Under Competing Models: Joint and Stepwise Approaches for Dynamic Cognitive Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06804)
*Yawen Ma,Sahoko Ishida,Kate Cain,Gabriel Wallin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了动态认知诊断中Q矩阵估计方法的选择对学习评估结论的影响，证明了在项目映射不明确的情境下，联合估计优于分步估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数字学习环境中，直接从细粒度响应数据推断学习进度时，Q矩阵（即各题目测量何种潜在技能的矩阵）往往是未知的。研究旨在探讨如何处理未知的Q矩阵（联合估计与分步估计），并分析这种选择对学习进度评估结论的影响。

Method: 研究采用了动态认知诊断模型（Dynamic Cognitive Diagnostic Models, DCDM），利用基于项目文本嵌入（Item-text embeddings）的先验信息来处理未知的Q矩阵。研究对比了“联合估计法”（Joint analysis）和“偏差校正后的分步估计法”（Bias-corrected stepwise analysis），并结合模拟研究验证了两种方法的差异及适用条件。

Result: 研究发现两种分析方法虽在学习者向精通技能发展的总体趋势上达成一致，但在对三年级仍处于“部分精通”状态的学习者数量估算上存在分歧。模拟研究进一步指出，当项目-技能映射不确定性较高或跨年级项目库发生变化时，联合分析能提供更可靠的参数估计结果。

Conclusion: 在评估学习者技能发展时，Q矩阵（项目-技能映射）的估计方式（联合估计与分步估计）对结论有实质性影响。在项目-技能结构不确定且项目库随时间变化的情况下，联合分析比分步分析更可靠、更具稳健性。

Abstract: Digital learning environments record learners' responses to individual items, making it possible to study the development of specific skills rather than overall scores. Drawing conclusions about learning from these data requires a model that links responses to latent skills and tracks how mastery changes over time. When the skills measured by each item are unknown, the analyst must decide whether to estimate this structure, the Q-matrix, jointly with the learning process, or to establish it first and study learning afterwards. We show that this decision can change substantive conclusions about how learners develop. Using dynamic cognitive diagnostic models, we analyse data from two reading games measuring vocabulary and comprehension from Grade 2 to Grade 3, with item-text embeddings providing prior information for the unknown Q-matrix. A joint analysis and a bias-corrected stepwise analysis agree that most learners move toward mastering both skills, but disagree about how many remain only partially proficient at Grade 3, changing how reading progress would be reported. A simulation study identifies when the two analyses diverge and shows that joint analysis is more reliable when the item-skill structure is uncertain and the item pool changes between grades. We provide R code for both analyses.

</details>


### [142] [SCALE: Scalable Cross-Attention Learning with Extrapolation for Agentic Workflow Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06820)
*Zhifei Xu,Jierui Lan,Zixuan Liang,Aiji Liang,Jinxi He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SCALE的DRL调度器，通过交叉注意力网络和结构化表征正则化（SRR），实现了对动态集群规模的通用调度，解决了传统方法在扩展规模时需要重新训练的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型（LLM）Agent系统任务调度器通常基于深度强化学习（DRL），但这些调度器往往绑定于固定的集群规模，一旦服务器数量变化就需要重新训练，难以适应动态变化的计算资源环境。因此，迫切需要一种能够泛化到未见集群规模且无需微调的DRL调度方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为SCALE的深度强化学习（DRL）调度器。该方法采用基于交叉注意力（Cross-Attention）的指针网络架构，使得模型能够天然地适应任意数量的服务器。此外，为了克服随规模增加而产生的特征分布偏移，作者引入了结构化表征正则化（SRR），通过解相关损失函数和KL散度惩罚，保持特征统计量在不同规模下的稳定性。

Result: 实验表明，在16个节点上训练的SCALE调度器，在直接测试于32和48个节点的集群时表现优异。特别是在N=48时，相比不带SRR的架构，SCALE将平均响应时间降低了8.9%，验证了其在跨规模调度任务上的高效性和稳健性。

Conclusion: 通过引入结构化表征正则化（SRR），SCALE有效地解决了DRL调度器在扩展集群规模时遇到的分布偏移问题，实现了在无需微调的情况下对未见集群规模的良好泛化，证明了在设计可扩展模型时，除了架构上的置换不变性，显式正则化对于保持特征统计稳定性至关重要。

Abstract: Agentic Large Language Model (LLM) systems decompose complex tasks into workflow Directed Acyclic Graphs (DAGs) whose primitives must be scheduled on heterogeneous clusters. Existing deep reinforcement learning (DRL) schedulers are tied to a fixed cluster size and require retraining whenever the number of servers changes. We propose SCALE (Scalable Cross-Attention Learning with Extrapolation), a DRL scheduler that generalizes to unseen cluster scales without fine-tuning. SCALE employs a cross-attention pointer network where task features query against server features, so the architecture accepts any number of servers by construction. We observe, however, that permutation-invariant architecture alone does not guarantee good performance at new scales - the attention feature undergoes distribution shift as the server count grows. To counter this, we introduce Structured Representation Regularization (SRR): a decorrelation loss combined with a KL penalty toward the standard normal, which keeps feature statistics stable regardless of input size. Trained on 16 nodes and tested directly on 32 and 48 nodes, SCALE reduces average response time by 8.9% at N=48 relative to the same architecture without SRR, confirming that explicit regularization is necessary to close the scale-generalization gap.

</details>

Unlike traditional models that optimize isolated prediction metrics, \textbf{PandaAI} is designed as a neuro-symbolic agent that navigates the complex, real-world financial environment with explicit risk awareness. ### [144] [Architecture Shapes Transfer Specificity in Implicit Neural Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06827)
*D Yang Eng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过受控实验对比了 SIREN、ReLU 和傅里叶特征 MLP 在坐标网络迁移学习中的表现，指出“迁移幅度”并不能完全反映模型学到了特定结构。研究强调在科学机器学习中，应引入“迁移特异性”作为诊断指标，而非单纯追求迁移增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 坐标网络中的迁移学习通常以“热启动增益”来衡量，但该指标无法明确区分增益是源自于任务特有的结构信息，还是仅仅源于通用的权重重用。作者旨在探究不同 INR 架构在处理科学机器学习任务时的迁移机制，并验证这种增益的本质。

Method: 研究采用了对照分析测试（包括独立随机种子对照、相同家族架构源对照）和消融实验。实验对象涵盖了三种主要的隐式神经表示（INR）架构：SIREN、ReLU MLP 和傅里叶特征 MLP。应用场景包括 2D 顶盖驱动流（Navier-Stokes）基准测试以及一系列 1D 偏微分方程（热方程、粘性 Burgers 方程、非线性薛定谔方程）。此外，文章还评估了现有的启发式缩放定律。

Result: 1. 迁移幅度和迁移特异性是两个独立维度。ReLU 展现出较高的特异性（对源任务更敏感），而 SIREN 虽然迁移幅度大，但往往表现出更广泛的权重重用。
2. 没有单一架构在所有 PDE 任务中占优。
3. 现有的静态诊断方法效果有限，且实验否定了启发式缩放定律 $A_{\text{transfer}} \propto 1/\Delta t^2$。

Conclusion: 研究表明，评估坐标网络（INR）的迁移能力时，不应仅依赖“热启动增益”（transfer magnitude），而必须考虑“迁移特异性”（transfer specificity）。架构的选择应在受控条件下进行评估，以区分模型是学习到了特定任务的结构，还是仅仅利用了通用的权重重用。

Abstract: Transfer in coordinate networks is often measured by warm-start gain, but whether that gain reflects source-specific structure or generic weight reuse is less clear. We study this question across three implicit neural representation (INR) families, SIREN, ReLU MLPs, and Fourier-feature MLPs, using controlled analytic tests, a 2D lid-driven-cavity Navier--Stokes benchmark, and 1D PDE reference-solution suites for heat, viscous Burgers, and focusing cubic NLS. The analytic tests use independent-seed random controls, while the PDE benchmarks use alternate same-family source controls and auxiliary ablations.
  Across settings, transfer magnitude and transfer specificity separate clearly. In a 10-seed controlled 1D geometric test, Fourier Features show the largest structured transfer ($33.1\times$), followed by SIREN ($23.0\times$) and ReLU ($10.7\times$), but ReLU is far more selective: random-control transfer is $0.41\times$ for ReLU versus $14.24\times$ for SIREN. On a controlled two-parameter 1D family, the ranking changes: ReLU gives the clearest structured-versus-control separation at default settings, whereas Fourier Features improve only after bandwidth retuning. In Navier--Stokes and the broader 1D PDE suite, no single architecture dominates every equation, yet the same pattern remains: SIREN often reuses weights broadly, whereas ReLU and, in some equations, Fourier Features are more source-selective. Static diagnostics remain weak, and the heuristic scaling law $A_{\text{transfer}} \propto 1/Δt^2$ is rejected in the implemented 1D audit.
  These results position transfer specificity as a useful diagnostic for coordinate networks and suggest that architecture selection in scientific machine learning should be evaluated under explicit control conditions, not by transfer magnitude alone.

</details>

TL;DR: 该论文提出了乘积单元残差网络（PURe），通过在架构中引入乘法单元来显式捕捉非线性特征交互，有效提升了模型在鲁棒性、样本效率和可解释性方面的表现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Understanding nonlinear feature interactions is crucial in science and engineering, yet standard multilayer perceptrons (MLPs) often capture such interactions only implicitly, leading to entangled representations that can impair robustness and interpretability. Beyond accuracy, SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP)-based interaction analyses show that PURe learns more concentrated and structurally coherent interaction patterns than MLP baselines. Overall, PURe achieves competitive or improved performance, better robustness and sample efficiency in low-data regimes, and enhanced interaction-level interpretability.

### [149] [Evidence-Grounded Ensemble Diagnosis of 802.11 Packet Captures: A Multi-Stage Pipeline with Deterministic Reliability Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06871)
*Jerome Henry,Swadhin Pradhan,Miroslav Popovic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 在 Wi-Fi 协议诊断中的幻觉和不可靠问题，PROBE 提出了基于确定性规范化、多模型集成和证据驱动推理的架构，实现了高精度、可验证且去偏的自动化诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人工 802.11 数据包诊断存在效率低、不一致且难以扩展的问题；而现有的 LLM 方法存在幻觉（编造协议事件）、缺乏校准的置信度评分，以及在评估过程中存在由模型本身生成的循环偏差问题。

Method: 1. PCAP-to-text 的确定性规范化：实现帧级可验证性；2. 多阶段集成推理：通过多运行、多候选模型获取第二意见，并采用渐进式混淆技术；3. 证据框架：将“缺失故障证据”本身视为证据的一部分进行处理；4. 确定性可靠性评分：基于证据有效性、运行稳定性与模型间一致性，而非模型自评，生成最终诊断结果。

Result: PROBE 框架在 87 个企业级 Wi-Fi 捕获数据集上实现了 0.957 的加权证据 F1 分数，显著高于专家基准（0.871），达到了 96% 的自动接受率，并有效消除了模型自评置信度高且不准确的现象。同时，其评估框架成功消除了循环评估偏差。

Conclusion: PROBE 框架通过整合确定性规范化、基于证据的集成推理以及不依赖 LLM 自我评估的可靠性评分机制，有效解决了 LLM 在 802.11 数据包诊断中的幻觉、过度自信及评估偏差问题，实现了高准确率且可信的自动化诊断。

Abstract: Diagnosing 802.11 packet captures requires expert protocol knowledge, is slow, inconsistent across engineers, and unscalable. LLM-based approaches sound plausible but fabricate protocol events absent from captures (especially truncated traces), produce uncalibrated confidence scores, and suffer evaluation bias when golden references are co-produced by the model under test. We introduce PROBE (Protocol Reasoning Over evidence-Based Ensembles), a multi-stage pipeline addressing all three failures. It integrates (i) deterministic PCAP-to-text normalization with frame-level verifiability, (ii) multi-run, multi-candidate ensembles with optional cross-model second opinion and progressive obfuscation, (iii) a verdict-aware evidence framework treating absence of failure evidence as contributing evidence, and (iv) a fully deterministic composite reliability score from evidence validity, run-to-run stability, and cross-model agreement without LLM self-assessment.
  On 87 enterprise Wi-Fi captures (104 capture-reviewer pairs), single-pass LLM analysis raises weighted evidence F1 from 0.871 (expert baseline) to 0.912 but misses critical frames in 35% of cases. Naive ensemble voting drops below baseline (0.842) as majority voting amplifies conservative verdicts: 50% of confirmed failures are misclassified as 'no issue' or 'insufficient evidence.' Adding evidence-grounded reconciliation achieves 0.957 F1, a 96% auto-accept rate, and a worst-case floor above 0.70. LLM self-reported confidence clusters at 0.95 regardless of difficulty (71% report exactly 0.95), confirming it is uninformative. We also introduce a model-agnostic evaluation framework using per-field assertion matching, eliminating circular bias from model-co-produced golden references.

</details>


### [150] [GlucoFM-Bench: Benchmarking Time-Series Foundation Models for Blood Glucose Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06881)
*Baiying Lu,Zhaohui Liang,Ryan Pontius,Shengpu Tang,Temiloluwa Prioleau*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 GlucoFM-Bench，这是一个评估血糖预测领域时间序列基础模型（TSFM）的综合基准平台。研究发现预训练模型在低数据量环境下表现优异，但在高数据量环境下传统轻量级模型仍占优势，并指出了针对极端血糖事件预测的持续改进需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 血糖预测对于糖尿病管理至关重要，但现有模型在处理不同糖尿病人群的异质性生理动态时面临挑战。尽管深度学习在预测方面已有应用，但新兴的时间序列基础模型（TSFM）在该领域的潜力尚未得到充分评估。该研究旨在通过构建基准测试，填补基础模型在血糖预测中的应用研究空白。

Method: 研究人员提出了 GlucoFM-Bench 基准测试平台，评估了八种代表性架构（包括预训练 TSFM、时间序列大语言模型和特定任务深度学习模型）。评估范围涵盖 15 个公开数据集，涉及 1,117 名受试者，并采用零样本、少样本和全样本训练协议，系统地考察了不同上下文长度和预测视界下的模型性能。

Result: 实验结果显示，Chronos-2 和 TimesFM 等预训练 TSFM 在零样本和少样本迁移学习中表现强劲，其零样本表现仅比最优全样本监督模型差 5%。然而，在数据充足的情况下，轻量级 LSTM 模型仍能超越 TSFM 4% 至 21%。此外，模型在 1 型糖尿病（T1D）群体及极端血糖区间的预测表现仍有待提升。

Conclusion: GlucoFM-Bench 为血糖预测领域建立了一个标准化的评估框架。研究表明，虽然预训练的时间序列基础模型（TSFM）在零样本和少样本场景下表现出色，但在拥有大量特定任务数据时，轻量级模型（如LSTM）仍具优势。未来的研究需要超越单一的聚合误差指标，重点关注对极端血糖水平（低血糖/高血糖）的预测能力。

Abstract: Blood glucose forecasting models are foundational for modern diabetes management systems, as reliable short-term predictions can enable proactive interventions, support automated insulin delivery, and reduce the risk of hypo- and hyperglycemic events. From a modeling perspective, glucose forecasting poses unique challenges due to heterogeneous physiological dynamics across diabetes populations. Traditional machine learning and deep learning models have been extensively evaluated for glucose prediction, yet recent time-series foundation models (TSFMs) remain much less studied in this setting. To bridge this gap, we present GlucoFM-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark evaluating state-of-the-art TSFMs alongside supervised deep learning models for blood glucose forecasting. We assess eight representative architectures, including pre-trained TSFMs, time-series large language models, and task-specific deep learning models, across 15 publicly available diabetes-relevant datasets comprising 1,117 individuals with type 1 diabetes, type 2 diabetes, prediabetes, and no diabetes. Models are evaluated under zero-shot, few-shot, and full-shot protocols, with systematic variation in context length and prediction horizon. Across datasets, pre-trained TSFMs, especially Chronos-2 and TimesFM, show strong zero-shot and few-shot transfer, with the best zero-shot model performing within 5% of the best full-shot supervised model. Yet, when task-specific data are abundant, a lightweight LSTM remains strongest, outperforming TSFMs by 4--21% under full-shot training. Stratified analyses reveal persistent challenges in T1D cohorts and hypo-/hyperglycemic ranges, highlighting the need for evaluation beyond aggregate error metrics. Together, GlucoFM-Bench provides a standardized and reproducible foundation for evaluating, comparing, and improving foundation models for blood glucose forecasting.

### [151] [Data-Constrained Language Model Pretraining: Improved Regularization and Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06888)
*Zhiwei Xu,Shihao Wu,Hanseul Cho,Wei Hu,Yixin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 随着高质量数据枯竭，语言模型预训练进入数据受限阶段。该研究提出了一种名为MIR的掩码辅助正则化方法以提升性能，并构建了SoftQ缩放定律，能更精准地指导有限数据下的模型缩放与多轮训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的预训练计算资源增长速度超过了高质量自然语言数据的供应速度，导致预训练即将进入“数据受限、计算资源充裕”的阶段（即模型需在有限数据集上进行多轮训练）。传统的Chinchilla缩放定律在假设数据无限、单次遍历数据集的前提下建立，无法准确指导这一新背景下的模型训练与扩展。

Method: 1. 正则化方法：引入掩码输入正则化（MIR），在自回归预训练基础上增加一个对随机掩码输入进行下一词预测的辅助损失函数。
2. 缩放定律：提出SoftQ缩放定律，通过耦合模型参数量和数据量来建模重复使用有限数据集下的性能，取代了传统Chinchilla定律中将两者解耦的加性形式。
3. 实验验证：在72M至1.4B参数规模的模型上，对比MIR与仅使用强权重衰减的方法，并对比SoftQ与传统缩放定律的拟合效果。

Result: 1. MIR能够有效提升模型在验证集上的性能，且在1.4B参数模型中，在下游任务中表现出显著增益。
2. 实验表明，MIR带来的性能提升相当于额外增加了约1.3倍的唯一训练数据。
3. SoftQ缩放定律在数据受限的实验环境下，其拟合效果显著优于传统的Chinchilla等缩放定律。

Conclusion: 该研究证明在数据受限的预训练场景下，通过引入掩码输入正则化（MIR）和采用新的SoftQ缩放定律，可以有效提升模型性能。MIR证明了类似扩散模型的掩码机制能为自回归模型带来额外增益，而SoftQ定律则比传统的Chinchilla定律更准确地描述了模型在多轮训练（多epoch）数据下的表现。

Abstract: Classical scaling laws for language model pretraining balance model size against training dataset size under a fixed compute budget, assuming abundant data and a single pass over the corpus. As training compute grows faster than the supply of natural language data, pretraining is likely to enter a data-constrained, compute-rich regime where models train for multiple epochs over a finite dataset. We study data-constrained pretraining along two axes, regularization and scaling. For regularization, we study masked-input regularization (MIR), an auxiliary next-token prediction loss on randomly masked inputs. MIR tests whether the random masking central to diffusion language models can benefit autoregressive pretraining without architectural changes or inference overhead. Across 72M to 1.4B parameter models, we find that MIR added on top of strong weight decay improves validation loss over autoregressive strong-weight-decay-only models, with downstream gains at 1.4B. For scaling, we propose SoftQ, a scaling law that couples model size and data size to capture their interaction under repeated data. Classical alternatives such as the Chinchilla law use an additive form that decouples these terms, making them misspecified in the data-constrained regime. We find that SoftQ fits data-constrained experiments substantially better than these alternatives, and estimates MIR's gains as equivalent to roughly 1.3 times as much unique training data. We release our code at https://github.com/yixinw-lab/dc_pretrain.

</details>


### [152] [GRASP: Geometry-aware Residual Alignment for Scalable Pretraining Data Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06892)
*Yue Min,Ruining Chen,Yujun Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 GRASP，一种考虑数据子集交互作用（如冗余与互补）的高效归因方法，通过二次几何惩罚与特征草图技术，在大幅降低计算成本的同时，显著提升了数据筛选和归因的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大多数可扩展数据归因方法将训练样本视为孤立个体并赋予效用分数，忽视了数据之间的冗余和互补性等关键子集动态（subset dynamics），导致在复杂数据集评估中表现不佳。因此，需要一种能够捕捉数据交互作用且具备预训练规模效率的新方法。

Method: 提出了 GRASP (Interaction-aware Surrogate) 方法，将数据归因重新定义为子集级反事实效用预测。该方法利用二次几何惩罚来明确建模数据间的交互作用，并通过低维特征草图（feature sketches）和有限下置信界（finite lower-confidence bound）选择协议，实现了大规模数据集上的高效计算。

Result: 在子集重训练评估中，GRASP 显著优于现有的可扩展基线方法；在反事实子集保真度任务中，其任务级秩相关性提升了两倍以上；同时，计算成本降低了近一个数量级。此外，该方法在语言模型策展和跨领域视觉数据筛选任务中表现出良好的迁移性和诊断能力。

Conclusion: GRASP 是一种能够有效捕捉数据子集交互作用的归因方法，通过引入二次几何惩罚和低维特征草图，在保持预训练规模效率的同时，显著提升了数据筛选和模型诊断的准确性，为大规模预训练数据的优化奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Scalable data attribution methods typically assign isolated utility scores to individual training examples. This prevalent additive assumption fundamentally fails to capture critical subset dynamics, including data redundancy and complementary coverage. In this work, we reframe attribution as subset-level counterfactual utility prediction and introduce GRASP, an interaction-aware surrogate. Grounded in a theoretical smoothness lower bound, GRASP explicitly models subset interactions through a quadratic geometric penalty. To achieve pretraining-scale efficiency without relying on hidden oracle tuning, we couple low-dimensional feature sketches with a strictly finite lower-confidence bound selection protocol. Extensive subset-retraining evaluations demonstrate that GRASP decisively outperforms existing scalable baselines. It more than doubles the task-level rank correlation for counterfactual subset fidelity while reducing upfront artifact construction costs by nearly an order of magnitude. Downstream diagnostics further show that this scoring mechanism transfers to language model curation and cross-domain vision selection, establishing a robust foundation for optimizing massive pretraining corpora.

### [153] [TALAN: Task-Aligned Latent Adaptation Networks for Targeted Post-Training of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06902)
*Chengkai Zhang,Ziteng Liu,Junpu Wang,Zeyi Tao,Yang Wang,Sagar Chordia,Qin Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TALAN 是一种创新的神经网络适配技术，通过在 Transformer 残差流中增加一个轻量级的“潜在侧路”，实现了序列感知的动态激活干预。它能与 LoRA 协同训练，在保持极低计算开销的同时，显著提升模型在复杂逻辑与编程任务上的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的低秩适配器（如 LoRA）虽然高效但缺乏任务感知能力，而现有的激活干预方法通常需要独立的探测器、向量或推理时引导。为了在不损失模型原有能力的前提下，提升模型在推理、数学和代码任务上的表现，作者希望开发一种既具备输入感知能力，又能在统一训练框架下高效实现的适配方法。

Method: 作者提出了 TALAN（任务对齐的潜在适配网络），这是一种序列条件化的潜在侧路架构，被插入到 Transformer 的残差流中。它与低秩适配器在一次监督微调（SFT）循环中联合训练，通过将活跃序列压缩为潜在记忆，将其重新混合为词元级的扰动，并利用受控的残差更新将其写回。该方法通过位置、记忆大小、混合器等六个维度进行配置。

Result: 在 Qwen3 系列模型和四个 STEM/代码基准测试中，TALAN 优于 LoRA 和 DoRA 基准。与 LoRA 搭配时，平均性能提升 1.41 个点；与 DoRA 搭配时，提升 1.85 个点。TALAN 仅增加了不到 1% 的可训练参数，且推理延迟极低（1.01-1.02x），显示出良好的实用性与扩展性（在 Llama-3.2 上也得到了验证）。

Conclusion: TALAN 提供了一个高效且实用的框架，能够将特定任务的激活干预与低秩适配器（LoRA/DoRA）协同训练，在几乎不增加推理成本和参数量的情况下，显著提升模型在推理、数学和编程任务上的表现。它验证了在标准适配器训练框架内实现可控的、序列感知的激活级适配的可能性。

Abstract: Targeted post-training aims to improve reasoning, math, and code without degrading strengths. Low-rank adapters are efficient but task-global; activation interventions are input-aware but often require separate probes, vectors, or inference-time steering. We introduce TALAN (Task-Aligned Latent Adaptation Networks), a sequence-conditioned latent side path inserted into a transformer's residual stream and co-trained with a low-rank adapter in one SFT loop. TALAN compresses the active sequence into latent memory, remixes it into token-level perturbations, and writes them back through a controlled residual update. It is configured along six axes: insertion location, memory size, mixer, writeback rule, trainability scope, and gradient scale.
  Across four Qwen3-family backbones and four STEM/code benchmarks, TALAN improves matched LoRA and DoRA baselines. With LoRA, it yields a +1.41 point cross-model mean gain, positive on all four backbones and non-negative on all 16 model-benchmark cells. With DoRA, it yields a +1.85 point mean gain, positive on all backbones and on 13 of 16 cells. Paired seed checks support positive average effects but show nontrivial variance, so we treat them as sensitivity checks. Cost is small: <1% trainable parameters relative to the backbone and 1.01-1.02x inference overhead versus matched LoRA. A Llama-3.2-1B transfer probe is also positive under LoRA and rsLoRA across seven paired seeds, supporting a transfer beyond Qwen.
  Internal-state analyses suggest TALAN is a small complementary activation intervention. The matched adapter update is 80-1,700x larger than the TALAN perturbation, yet their directions have near-zero cosine; per-layer measurements show this small orthogonal perturbation propagates and amplifies through depth. TALAN offers a practical platform for studying steerable activation-level adaptation within standard adapter-based post-training.

</details>


### [154] [The Fine-Tuning Trap: Evaluating Negative Transfer and the Role of PEFT in Sub-1B Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06920)
*Rahul Nair,Chun Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究指出，针对参数小于300M的小语言模型，全参数微调会导致严重的性能衰退；提出PEFT（LoRA/DoRA）是这类模型微调的稳定选择，并建议500M以下模型应禁用全参数微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在边缘设备上部署小语言模型时，现有的微调策略往往会导致模型通用能力下降。研究旨在探讨针对超小型模型（<1B）最高效且稳定的微调策略，并揭示全参数微调在极端小型化模型中存在的性能退化问题。

Method: 通过基准测试评估了五种参数量在135M至1B之间的小语言模型（SLM）在数学推理任务中的表现。对比了全参数微调（Full FT）与参数高效微调（PEFT，包括LoRA和DoRA）的性能差异，并将其与零样本（Zero-shot）和少样本（Few-shot）上下文学习效果进行了横向对比。

Result: 研究发现全参数微调对300M参数以下的模型具有显著负面影响（即“负迁移”），性能甚至低于零样本基准。在aligned模型中，LoRA表现优于全参数微调；对于极小型架构（如SmolLM2-135M），简单的少样本上下文学习效果优于全参数微调。此外，DoRA在复杂推理任务中表现更佳，而LoRA在模式匹配任务中更具优势。

Conclusion: 对于参数量小于500M的模型，应避免使用全参数微调（Full FT），以防止灾难性遗忘。对于所有经过对齐的小语言模型，应优先采用参数高效微调（PEFT）方法。选择LoRA还是DoRA取决于具体的任务类型（复杂推理选DoRA，模式匹配选LoRA）。

Abstract: Deploying Small Language Models (SLMs) on edge devices requires efficient fine-tuning strategies that adapt models to new tasks without degrading their general capabilities. In this study, we benchmark five sub-1B models (135M-1B) on mathematical reasoning tasks and uncover a critical vulnerability: Full Fine-Tuning (Full FT) actively harms performance in models under 300M parameters, often dropping accuracy below zero-shot baselines. This "negative transfer" makes Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) not just an efficiency preference, but a stability requirement. We find that while Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and Weight-Decomposed LoRA (DoRA) perform comparably, their strengths vary by task; DoRA excels in complex reasoning (GSM8K), while LoRA dominates pattern matching (OrcaMath). In particular, Full FT is outperformed by LoRA on aligned models (Qwen2.5-0.5B) and even by simple 5-shot In-Context Learning on the smallest architectures (SmolLM2-135M). Based on these findings, we recommend defaulting to PEFT for all aligned sub-1B models and caution against Full FT for any architecture smaller than 500M parameters to prevent catastrophic forgetting. Reproduction of this work can be found at https://github.com/gulguluu/tiny-slm-finetune-compare.

</details>


### [155] [From Sampled Outcomes to Capability Distributions: Rethinking Supervision for LLM Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06924)
*Guannan Lai,Haoran Hu,Long Chen,Zhenguo Li,Han-Jia Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出传统 LLM 路由依赖单次响应存在噪声，提出了 DARS 框架，利用输入和输出的分布特征来构建更可靠的路由监督信号，有效提升了模型选择的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 路由方法通常将模型的单次响应作为能力评估标签，但由于 LLM 生成的随机性，这种单次观测存在严重噪声，导致路由策略学习不可靠。

Method: 提出了 DARS (Distribution-Aware Routing Supervision) 框架。该方法不再依赖单次生成结果，而是通过考察输入端（语义等价的查询改写）和输出端（模型生成的随机性）的不确定性，构建分布式的能力估计，从而生成更可靠的路由监督信号。

Result: 实验表明，单次样本标注具有误导性；而基于 DARS 的分布式监督能够提供更稳定的标签，显著提升了路由模型的性能和决策稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了基于单次回复的路由监督存在系统性噪声，提出了 DARS 框架，通过引入分布感知的监督信号，证明了可靠的 LLM 路由应当从关注单次响应转向关注查询级别的模型能力分布。

Abstract: Existing LLM routing methods typically treat a model's single response to a query as its capability label for training routers. However, because LLM generation is inherently stochastic, such single-shot supervision provides only a noisy observation of a query-model pair's behavior rather than a reliable capability estimate. We show that this assumption introduces systematic noise into routing supervision, making learned routing policies less reliable. To address this issue, we propose DARS (Distribution-Aware Routing Supervision), a framework that constructs routing supervision from a distributional view of model behavior. Instead of relying on a single generated response, DARS considers uncertainty from both the input side and the output side, capturing how semantically equivalent query formulations and stochastic generations affect model performance. Based on these distribution-aware observations, DARS builds more reliable supervision signals for routing. Experiments across diverse tasks show that single-shot labels can be misleading for model selection, while distribution-aware supervision provides more stable labels and improves learned routing behavior. Our results suggest that reliable LLM routing should move beyond single-response observations and be grounded in query-level model capability distributions.

</details>


### [156] [Uniform Stability and Generalization Error of GD and SGD on Fixed-Point Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06934)
*Jonghyun Shin,Sejun Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文系统分析了离散参数空间（即引入舍入操作）对梯度下降算法的影响，发现确定性舍入会显著降低GD的泛化能力，而SGD则表现出更强的鲁棒性；同时揭示了随机舍入会导致泛化误差随维度增长的新现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的泛化理论大多假设参数空间为实数域，但在实际的硬件部署、量化训练或离散优化场景中，参数往往受到舍入操作的限制。论文旨在弥补这一空白，深入探究确定性舍入和随机舍入对梯度下降类算法泛化误差及稳定性的影响。

Method: 该论文运用了统计学习理论中的泛化误差分析、一致稳定性（Uniform Stability）以及一致参数稳定性（Uniform Argument Stability）框架。通过数学证明，对比了在确定性舍入和随机舍入策略下，梯度下降（GD）和随机梯度下降（SGD）在凸、Lipschitz连续且光滑损失函数上的泛化性能差异，并推导了上下界以验证理论结论。

Result: 1. 确定性舍入导致GD在凸、Lipschitz、光滑损失函数上的泛化误差从O(T/n)恶化至O(T/√n)，且GD的一致稳定性变为Ω(T)，导致基于稳定性的泛化界失效。
2. 确定性舍入下的SGD在同类损失函数上仍具有非平凡的一致稳定性，一维情况下为O(T/n)，高维情况下为O(T^2/n)。
3. 随机舍入引入了随维度增加而增加的泛化误差，这是实值优化和确定性舍入所没有的特性。
4. 给出了随机舍入策略下一致参数稳定性的紧致上界。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了离散参数空间下，舍入策略（确定性舍入与随机舍入）对梯度下降算法泛化性能的根本性影响。研究表明，确定性舍入破坏了GD的稳定性，使其泛化界失效，而SGD通过随机性能够维持一定的稳定性。此外，随机舍入引入了与维度相关的泛化误差，这种现象在实值优化中不存在。这些发现为在硬件限制或量化环境下使用优化算法提供了重要的理论指导。

Abstract: We analyze generalization error, uniform stability, and uniform argument stability of gradient descent (GD) and stochastic gradient descent (SGD) over discrete parameter spaces, where each update involves deterministic or stochastic rounding. We show that deterministic rounding degrades the generalization error of GD on convex, Lipschitz, and smooth loss functions, increasing the rate from $O(T/n)$ to $O(T/\sqrt{n})$, and establish matching lower bounds. We further prove that uniform stability of GD becomes $Ω(T)$, showing that stability-based generalization bounds are vacuous in this setting. In contrast, for the same losses, stochastic gradient descent with deterministic rounding admits nontrivial uniform stability guarantees, which differ qualitatively from the real-valued case and exhibit distinct dependencies on the number of iterations and the dimension: we prove tight bounds $O(T/n)$ for one dimension and $O(T^2/n)$ for higher dimensions. We also show that stochastic rounding can introduce generalization error that increases with the dimension; such a phenomenon is absent in standard real-valued optimization and in the deterministic rounding case. Finally, we provide upper bounds on uniform argument stability for stochastic rounding schemes and show that these bounds are tight when the loss can be represented as a sum of coordinate-wise functions.

</details>


### [157] [GenPO++: Generative Policy Optimization with Jacobian-free Likelihood Ratios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06967)
*Ke Hu,Shutong Ding,Panxin Tao,Jingya Wang,Ye Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GenPO++ 提出了一种高效的可逆生成式策略框架，通过高阶可逆 ODE 求解器实现了动作似然的精确、无 Jacobian 计算，消除了现有方法中的偏差和计算冗余，在复杂控制任务中展现了优异的性能和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于流（flow-based）的生成式策略在强化学习中应用存在局限：要么使用近似替代方案导致有偏更新，要么通过增加虚构动作（dummy-action）来计算精确似然，这不仅扩大了动作空间，还增加了计算成本。研究者希望在不引入偏差和额外计算开销的前提下，实现精确的似然计算。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GenPO++ 的可逆生成式策略优化框架。该方法利用历史状态作为辅助记忆，结合高阶可逆常微分方程（ODE）求解器，实现了动作空间无增维的精确逆映射。其核心在于将策略映射的对数行列式固定为求解器系数，从而实现无雅可比矩阵（Jacobian-free）的精确似然比计算。

Result: 在大型模拟控制、微调任务以及现实世界机器人操作任务中的实验表明，GenPO++ 在性能上达到或超过了现有的最先进在线强化学习方法，同时显著提升了训练稳定性和计算效率。

Conclusion: GenPO++ 通过创新的可逆 ODE 求解器设计，解决了生成式策略在强化学习中精确计算动作概率的难题。该方法不仅消除了偏差和额外的计算开销，还提升了复杂任务中策略的训练稳定性和性能，为生成式模型在强化学习中的应用提供了高效、精确的解决方案。

Abstract: Generative policies provide expressive and multimodal action distributions, making them attractive for reinforcement learning (RL) in complex continuous-control tasks. Among them, flow-based policies are especially appealing because they generate actions through deterministic transport maps. However, applying such generative policies to likelihood-based on-policy learning remains limited by the difficulty of evaluating the probability of executed actions. Existing flow RL methods either replace the true action-density ratio with approximate surrogates, which can introduce biased updates, or recover exact likelihoods through dummy-action augmentation, which enlarges the policy space and increases computation. In this work, we propose GenPO++, a reversible generative policy optimization framework that uses history states as auxiliary memory in a high-order reversible ODE solver, yielding exact inversion without changing the original action dimension. The resulting generative policy map has a log-determinant determined only by fixed solver coefficients, enabling exact and Jacobian-free likelihood-ratio computation. This design preserves the expressiveness of generative flow policies while avoiding both action ratio bias and dummy-action overhead. We evaluate GenPO++ on large-scale simulated control, fine-tuning, and real-world robotic manipulation tasks, where it achieves competitive or superior performance over state-of-the-art on-policy RL methods, while improving training stability and computational efficiency.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多目标贝叶斯优化（MOBO）在处理高昂计算成本的黑盒函数时，现有的获取函数往往存在收敛速度较慢的问题，尤其是在评估预算有限的情况下，需要更有效的手段来引导搜索。

Method: 提出了一种通用的加速机制，通过将高斯过程的预测梯度作为辅助信号引入到现有的多目标获取函数中。具体包括两种实现方式：一种是基于多梯度下降算法（MGDA）的自适应催化，另一种是预定义权重的变体，旨在限制预算条件下实现更高效的探索。

Abstract: This paper presents a general acceleration mechanism for multi-objective Bayesian optimisation (MOBO) that leverages Gaussian process predictive gradients as auxiliary signals. Rather than replacing existing Pareto-compliant acquisition functions, the proposed approach augments them with local stationarity information derived from surrogate-derived gradients, enabling faster convergence toward the global Pareto set under limited evaluation budgets. Two catalyst instantiations are investigated: an adaptive Multiple-Gradient Descent Algorithm-Based Catalyst (MGDA) and a predefined-weight variant that enables focused exploration when budgets are tight. Experiments on the DTLZ benchmark suite (using 2 objectives and 10 decision variables) show that predictive gradient catalysis can deliver significant acceleration compared to other acquisition functions (EHVI, AugTch, tMPoI, SAF) when surrogates are accurate, particularly for stationary problems.

### [161] [RASFT: Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning for Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07006)
*Yongliang Miao,Fengyuan Liu,Wei Shi,Yanguang Liu,Fei Sun,Na Zou,Mengnan Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RASFT 是一种自适应监督微调框架，它根据模型的实时表现动态调整对专家数据的模仿强度，既能在模型能力不足时通过专家引导强化学习，又能在模型能力成熟时鼓励自主推理，从而显著提升了模型在推理任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的监督微调（SFT）倾向于让模型机械模仿单一专家轨迹，这可能导致模型过拟合表面形式，抑制模型自身产生多样化逻辑推理的能力。

Method: 提出 Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning (RASFT) 框架：1. 根据在线验证的轨迹（Rollouts）评估问题难度和当前策略的掌握程度；2. 动态调节专家指导：策略较弱时强化引导，策略较强时降低模仿权重并引入模型自生成的正确轨迹；3. 引入基于冻结参考模型的截断逆比率约束，以防止策略过度偏离原有推理先验。

Result: 在六个数学推理数据集和两个代码推理数据集上的实验表明，RASFT 在性能上优于标准的 SFT、其他 SFT 变体以及代表性的强化学习方法。

Conclusion: RASFT 提出了一种更灵活的监督微调范式，证明了在推理任务中，动态调整专家引导的强度（根据策略的当前能力）优于传统的强制模仿，为大语言模型的推理能力提升提供了更高效的训练策略。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is a prevailing method for adapting large language models to reasoning tasks by imitating offline expert demonstrations, often treating a single expert trajectory as the target behavior. However, reasoning is not simple path imitation: rigidly following one demonstrated solution may overfit to surface forms and suppress the model's own reasoning distribution. We propose Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning (RASFT), a policy-aware SFT framework that calibrates expert supervision according to problem-level solvability estimated from verified on-policy rollouts. For each problem, RASFT strengthens expert guidance when the current policy struggles, while relaxing rigid imitation and incorporating correct self-generated trajectories when the model already exhibits reliable reasoning behavior. To preserve useful reasoning priors, RASFT further introduces a clipped inverse ratio between the frozen reference model and the current policy to constrain excessive policy drift. Experiments across multiple models on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks and two code reasoning benchmarks show that RASFT achieves better overall performance than SFT, SFT variants, and representative RL methods. The code is available at https://github.com/zjd1sq/RASFT.

</details>

Abstract: We propose a unified mathematical framework for a geometric understanding of concept learning and neuron interpretation in sparse autoencoders (SAEs). While SAEs improve interpretability of neural networks by learning sparse feature representations, a principled definition of ''concept'' and ''learning'' remains unclear. We formalize concepts as sets of data points and cast concept learning as a set-alignment problem between human-defined and model-induced concepts. This formulation distinguishes three increasingly strong notions of learning -- detection, separation, and approximation -- and yields geometric conditions, error bounds, and capacity constraints for when concepts can be represented by individual neurons or multi-neuron units. It also provides a set-theoretic account for common SAE phenomena, including feature splitting, feature absorption, feature families, and hierarchical concepts. Finally, we connect concept learning and neuron interpretation through formal concept analysis, showing that the two directions need not agree and that their many-to-many structure can be organized by concept lattices. ### [163] [CF-JEPA: Mask-free forward prediction with asymmetric encoder utilization for time-series representation learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07031)
*Jaehoon Lee,Sunghyun Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CF-JEPA 是一种创新的无掩码时间序列表示学习框架，它通过预测不同未来的时段来学习时序特征，并利用在线与目标编码器的固有差异，在分类、预测及异常检测等任务中取得了显著的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间序列自监督学习主要依赖对比学习（构造正负样本困难）和基于掩码的生成式学习（破坏时序连续性）。尽管 JEPA 方法避免了重构原始输入，但现有的时序 JEPA 变体仍严重依赖掩码，导致时序连续性被破坏。因此，作者旨在设计一种无掩码、利用时序本身固有顺序作为学习信号的新框架。

Method: 1. 提出 CF-JEPA 框架：摒弃了传统的掩码策略，改用多视界前向预测任务。
2. 采用截断数据（Crops）作为上下文视图，通过学习预测不同未来时段的表示（短、中、长期）来获取时序特征。
3. 利用在线编码器与 EMA 目标编码器的不对称性：在线编码器提取高秩判别性特征用于分类，EMA 目标编码器提取平滑的低秩时序特征用于预测和异常检测。

Result: 1. 在 126 个 UCR 和 26 个 UEA 分类数据集上，CF-JEPA 实现了自监督基线中的最高平均准确率。

3. 在单变量预测和异常检测任务中排名第二。
4. 验证了特征不对称性的有效性，实现了在无需额外训练开销下的任务自适应选择。

Conclusion: CF-JEPA 证明了在时间序列自监督学习中，无需掩码的预测任务同样有效，且能够通过利用在线编码器和 EMA 目标编码器之间的特征不对称性，实现针对不同下游任务的最优特征选择。这一方法在多个基准测试中表现优异，确立了其作为一种强有力的通用时间序列表示学习框架的地位。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning (SSL) for time-series representation learning is dominated by two paradigms: contrastive methods, which face challenges in constructing positive or negative pairs, and masking-based methods, which disrupt the temporal continuity of time-series signals. Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) offers a promising alternative by predicting in representation space rather than reconstructing raw inputs. However, existing time-series JEPA variants still rely on masking and therefore inherit its continuity problem. Crop-based Forward JEPA (CF-JEPA) is proposed as an innovative mask-free framework that replaces masking with multi-horizon forward prediction: random crops serve as context views, and short-, mid-, and long-horizon future representations are predicted in the forward temporal direction, directly leveraging the inherent temporal ordering of time-series data as a learning signal. A strong asymmetry is also identified between the online encoder and the exponential moving average (EMA) target encoder, both produced from a single training run: the online encoder develops higher-rank discriminative features, while the EMA target encoder develops smoother, lower-rank temporal features. Exploiting this asymmetry, classification is routed to the online encoder and forecasting or anomaly detection to the EMA target encoder, achieving a 27% reduction in multivariate forecasting mean squared error (MSE) at no additional training cost. Across 126 University of California, Riverside (UCR) and 26 University of East Anglia (UEA) classification datasets, eight electricity transformer temperature forecasting benchmarks, and Key Performance Indicator /Yahoo anomaly detection, CF-JEPA achieves the highest average accuracy and rank on UCR and UEA among self-supervised baselines and ranks second on univariate forecasting and k-nearest neighbors-scored anomaly detection.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市轨道交通中，车站客流与OD流之间存在内在的层次守恒关系，但现有研究通常将两者独立预测，导致结果不一致，无法满足实际运营决策需求。尤其在交通中断等突发情况下，这种不一致性更为严重，因此急需一种能保障分层一致性的联合预测方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为神经全连接协调器（Neural Fully Connected Reconciler, FCR）的框架。该方法通过学习从不一致的基础预测到一致的分层预测之间的非线性映射，利用神经网络的非线性建模能力，同时通过设计架构确保预测结果严格满足OD流与车站流之间的守恒约束。

Result: 实验表明，FCR框架在保证分层一致性的前提下，持续提升了OD流预测精度。在正常运营条件下，FCR表现与现有的MinT方法相当；在严重运营中断场景下，FCR显著优于传统统计方法，在多步目的地延误预测中将OD预测误差降低了高达17.45%。此外，预言机分析（Oracle analysis）表明提升车站级预测精度能显著改善整体预测效果。

Conclusion: 本文提出的分层协调框架有效解决了城市轨道交通客流预测中OD流与车站流不一致的问题，证实了分层协调机制在提升预测稳健性方面的有效性，特别是在运营中断等高压环境下表现优异，为城市交通的运营决策提供了更可靠的依据。

Abstract: Accurate and coherent passenger demand forecasting is essential for Urban Rail Transit (URT) operations. Passenger demand has a hierarchical structure in which origin-destination (OD) flows aggregate to station-level inflows and outflows through conservation constraints. In practice, station-level and OD-level forecasts are often generated independently, producing incoherent predictions that violate these constraints and introduce inconsistencies into operational decision-making. Such issues become more severe during disruptions, when forecasting reliability is most critical. This paper presents the first hierarchical forecast reconciliation framework for joint station-level and OD-level URT demand prediction. A neural Fully Connected Reconciler (FCR) learns a non-linear mapping from incoherent base forecasts to coherent hierarchical predictions while guaranteeing exact structural consistency by construction. The method is benchmarked against OLS, WLS, and Minimum Trace (MinT) variants using Rejsekort smart-card data from the Copenhagen S-train network under one-step, multi-step, and disruption forecasting scenarios. Results show that reconciliation consistently improves OD forecasting accuracy while ensuring hierarchical coherence. Under normal conditions, FCR performs competitively with MinT-based methods. An oracle analysis indicates that perfect station-level forecasts could reduce OD prediction error by up to 34 percent, highlighting the value of improved base forecasts. Under severe disruptions, FCR outperforms classical methods, reducing OD forecasting error by up to 17.45 percent in multi-step destination-side delay scenarios. These findings establish hierarchical reconciliation as an effective mechanism for improving forecast robustness, with the largest benefits occurring under the most challenging operating conditions.

</details>


### [165] [Constructing VAE Latent Spaces with Prescribed Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07058)
*Jilles S. van Hulst,Jakub M. Tomczak,W. P. M. H. Heemels,Duarte J. Antunes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对VAE中高斯先验与非欧几里得数据流形之间的拓扑失配问题，本文提出了一种数学框架，通过利用覆盖空间和商空间结构，构造出与数据拓扑相匹配的潜在先验，显著提升了模型在复杂流形数据上的表征和重建能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的变分自编码器（VAE）通常假设潜在空间遵循高斯先验，这种欧几里得拓扑假设与实际数据的非欧几里得流形结构存在拓扑失配（Topological Mismatch），导致重建质量下降且无法准确表征数据。

Method: 提出了一种基于乘积覆盖空间的数学框架。该方法将流形分解为基本因子（圆、区间或直线）或其有限对称群的商空间，并为这些因子配置相应的可重参数化分布。通过引入特定的坐标变换和锚点约束，使神经网络能够输出适配非欧几何的参数，同时确保解码器在商空间中保持群不变性。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在合成流形及旋转/循环位移的MNIST数据集上均优于高斯先验基准模型。在各种正则化强度下，拓扑匹配的先验均能更准确地对齐KL正则化与数据流形，显著提升了潜在空间的表征能力和重建质量。

Conclusion: 通过为特定的非欧几里得流形定制先验分布，研究证明了拓扑匹配对VAE性能的关键影响。这种方法不仅解决了拓扑失配问题，还通过解耦的KL散度保持了训练的高效性，为处理具有复杂几何结构的数据提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Variational autoencoders (VAEs) learn low-dimensional latent representations of high-dimensional data. When the data lies on a manifold with non-Euclidean topology, the standard Gaussian prior introduces a topological mismatch that degrades reconstruction quality and prevents faithful representation. We present a constructive mathematical framework that resolves this mismatch for all manifolds that admit a product covering space. These are manifolds expressible as products of elementary factors (circles, intervals, or lines) or as quotients of such products by a finite symmetry group. The class includes cylinders, tori, Möbius strips, Klein bottles, and real projective spaces. Factorized distributions over the elementary factors yield product topologies with closed-form, decoupled KL divergences, so that each latent factor can be shaped independently while keeping training tractable. We catalogue reparametrizable encoder-prior pairs for periodic, bounded, and unbounded supports, and provide coordinate transformations that allow standard neural networks to output non-Euclidean parameters with smooth gradients. For quotient manifolds, the decoder receives group-invariant features of the covering-space coordinates, so that identified points produce identical outputs. Anchor constraints fix the coordinate system relative to the data or create soft topological holes. Experiments on synthetic manifolds and real-image datasets (rotated and cyclically shifted MNIST) confirm that a topology-matched prior aligns KL regularization with the data manifold. The resulting topology-aware models outperform the Gaussian baseline at all practically relevant regularization strengths. The code is available at https://github.com/JvHulst/VAE-Topology.

</details>


### [166] [Bias in Filter Feature Selection Evaluation: A Meta-Analysis of Datasets, Baselines, and Experimental Design Choices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07068)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 多元线性回归分析显示，数据集数量、基准方法数量和新方法数量能够解释研究中新方法胜率变异性的33%（R²=0.33），证明评估设置对研究结论具有显著影响。

Conclusion: 特征选择方法的评估存在潜在偏见。评估结果受实验设置（如数据集数量、基准方法数量）影响，现有的评估范式需要更严谨、标准化的准则，以提升研究的可信度与公平性。

Abstract: Background: Since 1990 many feature selection methods have been proposed across heterogeneous applications. To validate the usefulness of a new method, it needs to be compared against at least one baseline method from the existing literature on a feature selection task using at least one dataset. Recent developments in tabular Deep Learning (DL) and data valuation in Machine Learning (ML) suggest that the evaluation of new methods, algorithms, and models may be consciously or unconsciously biased. We hypothesise that a similar trend exists in feature selection (FS), particularly in filter feature selection (FFS). The aim of this study is therefore to examine FFS studies to identify factors that influence the evaluation and that might consist entry point for biases in order to recommend stronger principles for FFS evaluation.
  Methods: We analyse a sample of 28 high profile FFS studies published between 1994 and 2025. The analysis provides reflections on how to examine FFS studies, highlights lessons learned throughout the process, and gives five evidence-based recommendations for future FFS evaluation.
  Results: Multivariate Linear Regression analysis achieved a score of $R^2=0.33$. It means that 33% of the variance in the performance of new methods against chosen baselines (win rate) is explained by the number of datasets (#Datasets), the number of baselines (#Baselines), and the number of new methods (#NewMethods).
  Discussion: $R^2=0.33$ is considered medium explanation; which is promising given that this is the first such study. The medium explanation result is due to the fact that win rate is influenced by additional factors such as the maturity of the feature selection domain, the type of datasets and baselines, and the simplicity of the regression model used to explain the relationship.

### [167] [SlimSearcher: Training Efficiency-Aware Web Agents via Adaptive Reward Gating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07074)
*Zequn Xie,Junjie Wang,Dan Yang,Jie Feng,Yue Shen,Jian Wang,Jinjie Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有深度搜索智能体在复杂任务中因盲目使用工具导致的冗余和高成本问题，SlimSearcher 通过在 SFT 和 RL 阶段引入帕累托高效过滤与自适应奖励门控机制，显著提升了模型的执行效率，实现了准确性与成本的 Pareto 最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的深度搜索智能体过于依赖暴力策略，表现为对工具的盲目使用和冗长的推理过程。这种以准确性为唯一导向的范式导致了计算资源的大量浪费（冗余轨迹和高昂的Token消耗），即所谓的“效率陷阱”。因此，研究者旨在构建一个能平衡准确性和计算成本的框架。

Method: 1. 帕累托高效过滤（Pareto-efficient filtration）：在有监督微调（SFT）阶段，筛选并利用既成功又经济的轨迹进行训练，使模型具备内在的效率意识。
2. 自适应奖励门控（Adaptive Reward Gating）：在强化学习（RL）阶段，通过评估采样群组内的相对工具和Token效率，动态进行奖励塑造，并通过严格的正确性门控避免奖励黑客攻击和简短偏差。

Result: 在 GAIA、BrowseComp 和 XBenchDeepSearch 等长跨度基准测试中，SlimSearcher 在保持或提升任务准确率的同时，平均工具调用轮次减少了 17% 至 58%。

Conclusion: SlimSearcher 提供了一种在保持甚至提升深层搜索任务准确性的前提下，显著降低计算成本和工具调用频率的有效方案。该研究表明，通过在模型训练阶段引入显式的效率感知机制，可以有效克服当前大模型在复杂任务中存在的“冗余推理”问题，为构建高效的智能体系统指明了方向。

Abstract: Deep research agents have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in complex information-seeking tasks, yet this power comes at a steep computational cost. Driven by accuracy-focused training paradigms, current models adopt brute-force strategies characterized by blind tool dependency and performative reasoning-generating long, redundant trajectories that are far from necessary for resolving these tasks, leading to wasteful tool calls and excessive token consumption. To overcome this efficiency trap, we propose SlimSearcher, a principled framework that pushes the Pareto frontier between accuracy and computational cost across both Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). In the SFT stage, SlimSearcher employs Pareto-efficient filtration to distill trajectories that are both successful and economical, guiding the model toward inherently efficiency-aware search behaviors. During RL, we introduce Adaptive Reward Gating, a dynamic reward-shaping mechanism that evaluates relative tool and token efficiency within a sampled cohort. By cascading these adaptive efficiency metrics with a strict correctness gate, our approach effectively avoids the brevity bias associated with absolute penalties and mitigates reward hacking. Extensive experiments on long-horizon benchmarks, including GAIA, BrowseComp, and XBenchDeepSearch, demonstrate that SlimSearcher reduces average tool-call rounds by 17%-58% while maintaining or improving accuracy.

### [168] [On the Geometry of On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07082)
*Zhennan Shen,Yanshu Li,Qingyu Yin,Chak Tou Leong,Zhilin Wang,Yanxu Chen,Rongduo Han,Sunbowen Lee,Yi R. Fung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分析参数空间动力学，揭示了在线策略蒸馏（OPD）具有独特的“子空间锁定”更新模式，其训练动态显著区别于 SFT 和 RLVR，且早期形成的低维更新子空间已足以维持其推理优化效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在线策略蒸馏（OPD）被广泛用于提升大语言模型的推理能力，但其背后的训练动力学机制尚不明确。研究者旨在通过分析 OPD 在参数空间中的更新轨迹，揭示其与 SFT 和 RLVR 等方法的本质区别，从而更好地理解和优化该训练范式。

Method: 研究团队采用了一套参数空间诊断工具，通过对比 OPD、SFT 和 RLVR 在更新轨迹、受影响权重数量、主方向偏离度以及累积更新的维数等方面的差异，分析其动力学行为。此外，通过控制实验（如稀疏化 token、改变 rollout 生成策略及混合目标函数）进一步验证了 OPD 更新子空间的稳定性与特异性。

Result: 研究发现：1. OPD 处于一种“松弛的非主方向（relaxed off-principal）”状态，相比 SFT，其影响的权重更少且更避开主方向；2. OPD 表现出“子空间锁定（subspace locking）”特性，即累积更新迅速收敛于一个狭窄的低维通道；3. 将 OPD 训练限制在早期形成的更新子空间内不会影响其性能，但会对 SFT 造成显著损害，证明该子空间对于 OPD 具有函数上的充分性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了在线策略蒸馏（OPD）在参数空间中具有独特的更新几何结构，并非简单的监督微调（SFT）与强化学习（RLVR）的中间形态。OPD 的训练动力学表现出明显的“子空间锁定”现象，即早期形成的低维更新通道足以支撑后续性能，这为高效模型微调和理解大模型推理优化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) is increasingly used to improve large language model reasoning, but its training dynamics remain poorly understood. We characterize the trajectory of OPD updates in parameter space and compare it with supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). A suite of parameter-space diagnostics consistently places OPD in a relaxed off-principal regime: compared with SFT, its updates affect fewer weights and avoid principal directions more strongly, while compared with RLVR, they remain less tightly constrained. Beyond this static localization, OPD exhibits subspace locking: its cumulative updates rapidly enter a narrow low-dimensional channel. Constraining training to the update subspace formed early in training preserves OPD performance but substantially degrades SFT, indicating that the locked subspace is functionally sufficient for OPD. Control experiments further show that sparsifying the update tokens and shifting rollout generation off-policy preserve the rank dynamics, whereas mixing the OPD objective with RLVR changes them. Overall, these results suggest that OPD is not merely an intermediate point between SFT and RLVR, but induces its own update geometry in parameter space.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了残差控制乘子学习（RCML）算法。该方法的核心思想是将投影乘子分解为用于原始下降的“有效压力信号”和用于有限增益乘子跟踪的“压力记忆残差”。此外，引入了模块化的随机稳定组件以处理异构和噪声观测。

Result: 在凸仿射框架下建立了有限增益收敛性，并导出了小批量反馈下的随机残差界。实验结果表明，RCML在优化、资源分配及公平排序任务中，不仅能维持竞争性的目标函数性能，还显著改善了可行性控制和乘子稳定性。
